Each password should be on a new line.\n\n3. **Run Hydra**:\n   - Use the following command to test passwords against an FTP server:\n   ```bash\n   hydra -l <username> -P <path/to/password/list.txt> ftp://<target_ip>\n   ```\n\n   - Replace `<username>` with the FTP username, `<path/to/password/list.txt>` with the path to your password list, and `<target_ip>` with the target FTP server's IP address.\n\n### Important Notes:\n- **Authorization**: Ensure you have explicit permission to test the FTP server.\n- **Testing Environment**: It's best to perform tests in a controlled environment, such as a test server that you own.\n- **Rate Limiting**: Be mindful of the server's rate limits to avoid being blocked.\n\nIf you have further questions about using Hydra"]}, "status": "in_progress", "end_turn": null, "weight": 1.0, "metadata": {"citations": [], "content_references": [], "gizmo_id": null, "message_type": "next", "model_slug": "gpt-4o-mini", "default_model_slug": "auto", "parent_id": "aaa2f033-91fd-452e-97e7-18545fd0763f", "model_switcher_deny": []}, "recipient": "all", "channel": null}, "conversation_id": "6706ebc7-5820-8011-9445-c37310aa047e", "error": null}
